<div id="review_310659575" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/310659575" />
    <a title="Kristy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2705039-kristy"><img alt="Kristy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1453228324p2/2705039.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/310659575?book_show_action=true">Apr 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristy" href="/user/show/2705039-kristy">Kristy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2705039-kristy?shelf=i-think-you-should-read-this">i-think-you-should-read-this</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer310659575" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13391811602546807867">Of Poseidon was not what I was expecting. From the title, I was thinking something along the lines of the Percy Jackson Poseidon and I didn’t get that at all. I got Mermaids! (oops sorry Syrena). I very much so enjoyed myself with this one. Yes, there was some cheese-tastic moments, but all in all I had a swimmingly good time…. < yep I just went there! <br/><br/>I have to note I think I would have been goo-goo-gaga crazy in love with this back in High School…. Being the old spinster that I am now, I did f</span>
  <span id="freeText13391811602546807867" style="display:none">Of Poseidon was not what I was expecting. From the title, I was thinking something along the lines of the Percy Jackson Poseidon and I didn’t get that at all. I got Mermaids! (oops sorry Syrena). I very much so enjoyed myself with this one. Yes, there was some cheese-tastic moments, but all in all I had a swimmingly good time…. &lt; yep I just went there! <br /><br />I have to note I think I would have been goo-goo-gaga crazy in love with this back in High School…. Being the old spinster that I am now, I did feel a little bit of disconnect…. But, I still enjoyed myself plenty.<br /><br />So, what’s this book about you ask?? At the core, it’s about Emma. Emma who just lost her best friend. Emma who has a bad temper. Emma who is clumsy. Emma who just bumped into Galen. Emma who has a secret, she doesn’t know about herself.<br /><br />Emma can communicate with fish, Galen witnessed that firsthand, but he needs to know if she is really a Syrena. If so, how has she survived so long as a human? How can she not like seafood? Why is he so drawn to her, and how can he make it stop, he knows she is not his to have. <br /><br />This book is littered with sexual tension and denial. Galen is such a corny, yet sexy beast! <br /><br />Beware if you read this, the ending is quite the cliffhanger/surprise and you will be foaming at the mouth for the next installment.<br /><br />3.5 stars <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13391811602546807867" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('w1Ip4A5zkXSG+fMjjsyWggGFVbNswt6tyRO8fAQALE1FzEDo0WzUxtvNQLnHy2HCRY+KlrA7+HDUkjRULNgJDw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kqpYwH4D1raToxCeRqb2jMdZ3LMqHpoN3OyS4ZvpU1MUNDHIoRyTBM6XowQPoQHMg1MDlvbnvNDBbRrJszF2EQ==')})
  }
//]]>
